<Time>1587668528523</Time><user_name>Sarah Coombs< /user_name><Text>I'm used to shopping at the big chain stores and wasn't sure what to expect on my first visit to A & A Textiles adorable little "hole-in-the-wall" fabric shop. I was pleasantly surprised to find this place well stocked with a huge variety of fabrics, and the prices are so reasonable (compared to what I am used to paying at JoAnnes) that I can afford to branch out into more sewing projects and have more fun behind my machine! But the thing that really blew me away and made me a lifetime customer was the care they provided to me when the Covid-19 pandemic hit and all the fabric shops closed. I was halfway through sewing a large amount of custom cloth dinner napkins for my upcoming wedding (I had a unique wedding color scheme and opted to sew matching napkins), and I ran out of fabric! I was devastated. I couldn't get any supplies anywhere, and I didn't have enough fabric at home to get the job done in time for my special day. I called A & A Textiles to ask when they would next be open to the public. The person I spoke to on the phone was extremely kind and sympathetic to my situation and arranged to have a gentleman, who I'm assuming was the store manager, meet me outside the closed store to help me acquire the fabric I so desperately needed. Thanks to the amazing level of compassion they showed me I was able to complete all the napkins for my wedding on time. They went above and beyond for me, and I'll never forget it. Thank you A & A Textiles, the best fabric shop in town!< /Text>< pictures>

<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
This was my first new patient appt. with Dr Bhadauria for a general pap- and I felt very seen and heard. Great first impression.

Specifically the nurse staff and Dr. Bhadauria were all very personable. They were engaging, made eye contact and I did not feel like just another number/patient.

The appointment ran on schedule (I was early/on time for paperwork) and did not have to wait long before being seen.

The front desk anticipated my needs by offering the location of bathroom if needed.

There were clear instructions, as well as verbal confirmations, about their insurance limitations in regards to in-house or send outs for lab testing.

I did ask the nurse many questions being a new patient in office - and was greeted with clarity and friendliness. Again - frequent eye contact :)

My most beloved take away was Dr. Bhadauria‚Äôs calm, sincere, and gentle grounding presence. She also conducted my health history herself, which is rare (and huge!) when you have a lengthy back history like myself. Ive only experienced this attentiveness with holistic doctors. So this dynamic definitely sent the message of  ‚Äúhands on‚Äù care. She was engaging in this regard and I felt very secure knowing the time was being taken to really hear and take notes about my current issues as well as past history and family history.

This also helped alleviate the exhausting process of repeating my health history to one staff member, then another, finally explaining once again to the doctor - and doing so in a summarized fashion feeling rushed.

I‚Äôve had ongoing chronic health issues and infections for upwards 10-12 yrs and as a result have seen and visited a myriad of doctors, specialists and consultants. So I am very familiar with the incredible downsides of the majority of doctor visit morale- ie: rushed appts, limited time with the doctor, emotionally/
mentally checked out staff /doctors, lack of sensitivity or third degree condescending responses, insurance transparencies, front desk disorganization or overt rudeness etc...you name it. Very pleased - this was not the case here.

I left feeling taken care of and confident I have finally found an OBGYN I can feel comfortable seeing in the future and one who wants to get to bottom of things as well.

Fun fact: I also left my cell phone by accident in the exam room and when I came back the receptionist was on a call. She signaled me, and quietly passed my phone over.  Seemless :)</Text>

After the nurse did all the prep, Dr. Bhaduaria came with a warm smile( I still see even if she is wearing mask) and warm greetings. She reviewed my medical history, provided information and reminded me the necessary screening for my age. Before doing the procedure, she explained what to expect step bu step. This is very important for the patient as a Gyn exam is not fun. After the exam, Dr. Bhadauria informed me that they will call as soon as the result came in. She also told me that she will give me a referral. The referral was sent to my email which I think is great. Lastly and the most importantly is their timely notification about the result of the exam. We all know that waiting for pending test result is nerve wracking, but Heather did not disappoint. She called me as soon as the result came back, which I really appreciate because I had a bad experience with physicians not calling their patients about an abnormal test results.<//Review>

< review>
I took my car to Boyd's for what appeared to be a radiator leak.  He told me they would inspect it, find what the problem was, and call me.  They looked at it, called me and told me I would need a New Radiator, and a new Thermostat.  They also told me my Coolant Sensor was bad, and needed to be replaced.  I authorized the repairs.  The repairs were done on time-  I was concerned about this, because I had to be at work in mid-afternoon.  The work was done on time, and he also gave me a big break on the cost of the parts.
Now, here is the bottom line:  the work was done in a timely, very professional way.  My car has not run this way in a long time.  I believe the car computer was running in a different mode, because of the faulty Coolant Sensor.  My very rough idle is gone, the car has a lot more power (it wants to get up and go now) and has  better gas mileage.
I would recommend Boyd's to anyone that wants quality work done at a reasonable price.  Go by and look at their parking lot.  You will find it very full, all the time.  They would not have all these cars if they did not do  good quality work, at a reasonable price.
Unfornatuately, I do not work up here in this area anymore.  I will drive the 50 miles, to bring my car in for repairs to Boyd's.  My sister's truck is running really bad.  I am working on it so we can drive it to Boyd's to have them find out what is wrong with it.  If not, I am going to have it towed to Boyd's.
I am completely 100% sold on Boyd's and would recommend them to anyone.  Floyd<//review>

However, at this moment, he talked fast and mean saying, "You go check the milage of your car, there's not even 1mi added!"  I noticed he was holding my car keys tighter, so I knew I wouldn't get my car back to work unless I paid him.  So he got it his way.

(2) Bob charged me storage fee but actually kept customers' cars on the st.  This is a small shop, yet it's in an unsafe area.  So they move customers' cars to the street after they fix them.

(3) They estimated 3 days to fix my bumper, but it took 7 days, causing car rental cost double....and what's better for them, they charged me STORAGE FEE using public streets! <text>(Translated by Google) Before ordering wine, the bartender will ask if you need "Open a tab", which means to keep the bill for you. If you are not only having a drink, then you can directly pass the credit card to him and tell him your name. Remember that the name must be the same as the name on the credit card. When you wait for the next glass of wine, tell him what your name is. The waiter will charge the fee from your credit card. Just go to "Close the tab" before you leave. Of course, in addition to using a credit card, cash can also be used to pay the bill. Don't worry that the bartender can't remember your name, they are very professional. If it is a bar with a lot of people, you may be given a number, and you only need to report the number to order. Speaking of wine, if you choose beer, most Bars will have their own beer selection. There are a variety of barrels of loose beer, which is directly connected to the tap. This is called "Beer on tap", except for For a cup, you can also choose to have a pitcher. This type of beer is generally at a good temperature, and you can taste a few more. Some beer bars will change the wine halfway. There are many choices. It is best to start with the lightest beer. Most light-colored beer will taste a little lighter, even It is fruity, but the safest way is to ask the waiter. There are many types of beer in the United States, mainly divided into two categories, Ale and Lager. Ale is top-level fermentation and belongs to high-temperature fermentation, while Lager is bottom-level low-temperature fermentation and has a lighter color. Most beers currently on the market belong to Lager.
